 HEADER                        DATA ELEMENT

 SRMP                          STATE ROUTE MILEPOST
 B                             STATE ROUTE MILEPOST AHEAD BACK INDICATOR
 ARM                           ACCUMULATED ROUTE MILE
 FEATURE                       LABEL
 DIRECTION TO INVENTORY        ROADWAY INVENTORY DIRECTION
 LEFT/RIGHT INDICATOR          ROADWAY LEFT RIGHT INDICATOR
 DESCRIPTION                   ROADWAY DESCRIPTION
 BRIDGE OW                     BRIDGE CROSSROAD OWNER CODE
 BRIDGE L                      BRIDGE ILLUMINATION INDICATOR
 UXING OW                      UNDER CROSSING CROSSROAD OWNER CODE
 UXING L                       UNDER CROSSING ILLUMINATION INDICATOR
 XROAD OW                      CROSSROAD OWNER CODE
 XROAD TC                      INTERSECTION TRAFFIC CONTROL TYPE
 XROAD L                       INTERSECTION ILLUMINATION INDICATOR
 WIDTH AND SURFACE INFORMATION
      NBR LNS D                ROADWAY DECREASING NUMBER OF LANES
      NBR LNS I                ROADWAY INCREASING NUMBER OF LANES
      DECREAS/DIV LFT SHD W/S  SHOULDER LEFT WIDTH / SHOULDER LEFT TYPE
      DECREAS/DIV RDY W/S      ROADWAY DECREASING WIDTH / ROADWAY DECREASING SURFACE TYPE
      DECREAS/DIV RHT SHD W/S  SHOULDER LEFT CENTER WIDTH / SHOULDER LEFT CENTER TYPE
      MEDIAN WD/S              MEDIAN WIDTH / MEDIAN TYPE
      MEDIAN BR                MEDIAN BARRIER TYPE
      INCRES/UNDI LFT SHD W/S  SHOULDER RIGHT CENTER WIDTH / SHOULDER RIGHT CENTER TYPE
      INCRES/UNDI RDW W/S      ROADWAY INCREASING WIDTH / ROADWAY INCREASING SURFACE TYPE
      INCRES/UNDI RHT SHD W/S  SHOULDER RIGHT WIDTH / SHOULDER RIGHT TYPE
      SPC USE LNS WID          SPECIAL USE LANE WIDTH
      TOT RDY WID              TOTAL ROADWAY WIDTH
 CLASSIFICATIONS
      MTCE A                   MAINTENANCE AREA NUMBER
      MTCE SE                  MAINTENANCE SECTION NUMBER
      CITY NBR                 CITY NUMBER
      ST FC                    RURAL/URBAN CODE / STATE FUNCTION CLASSIFICATION
      LEGAL SPEED D / IB       SPEED LIMIT LEGAL SPEED
      TR                       TERRAIN TYPE
      PK                       PARKING ZONE TYPE
      ST                       STREET NAME ALIAS DESCRIPTION
 TURN LANES
      L NEAR LGT / WD          TURN LANE LEFT NEAR LENGTH / TURN LANE LEFT NEAR WIDTH
      R NEAR LGT / WD          TURN LANE RIGHT NEAR LENGTH / TURN LANE RIGHT NEAR WIDTH
      L FAR LGT / WD           TURN LANE LEFT FAR LENGTH / TURN LANE LEFT FAR WIDTH
      R FAR LGT / WD           TURN LANE RIGHT FAR LENGTH / TURN LANE RIGHT FAR WIDTH
 ACCELERATION LANES
      LEFT LGT / WD            ACCELERATION LANE LEFT LENGTH /ACCELERATION LANE LEFT WIDTH
      L-CNTR LGT / WD          ACCELERATION LANE LEFT CENTER LENGTH / ACCELERATION LANE LEFT CENTER WIDTH
      R-CNTR LGT / WD          ACCELERATION LANE RIGHT CENTER LENGTH / ACCELERATION LANE RIGHT CENTER WIDTH
      RIGHT LGT / WD           ACCELERATION LANE RIGHT LENGTH / ACCELERATION LANE RIGHT WIDTH




 FOR DESCRIPTION AND DEFINITION OF DATA ELEMENTS, REFER TO THE "TRIPS USER GUIDE" , "DATA ELEMENT DEFINITIONS".  FOR ROADWAY DATA
 QUESTIONS, OR IF YOU CAN PROVIDE UPDATED ROADWAY INFORMATION, PLEASE CONTACT THE ROADWAY DATA OFFICE AT (360) 570-2361.
